<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>Apparently, the editors made the decision to swap several of the trombone and ophicleide (or tuba, in this case) parts in the fourth movement, completely eliminating the third trombone's infamous pedal tones.
</td></tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>

<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Symphonie fantastique
</td></tr>

</td></tr>

<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="zh-hans, zh-cn, zh-sg">幻想交响曲</span>; <span title="zh-hant, zh-hk, zh-tw, ja, zh">幻想交響曲</span>; <span title="pl">Symfonia fantastyczna</span>; <span title="eu">Sinfonia fantastikoa</span>; <span title="he">הסימפוניה הפנטסטית</span>; <span class="expandline" title="17 more..."><span title="es, gl">Sinfonía fantástica</span>; <span title="oc, it">Sinfonia fantastica</span>; <span title="hu">Fantasztikus szimfónia</span>; <span title="et">Fantastiline sümfoonia</span>; <span title="en, da">Symphonie Fantastique</span>; <span title="pt">Sinfonia Fantástica</span>; <span title="ru">Фантастическая симфония</span>; <span title="sr-el, sr">Fantastična simfonija</span>; <span title="sr-ec">Фантастична симфонија</span>; <span title="th">แซ็งฟอนีฟ็องตัสติก</span>; <span title="ca">Simfonia fantàstica</span>; <span title="fi">Fantastinen sinfonia</span>; <span title="uk">Фантастична симфонія</span>; <span title="cs">Fantastická symfonie</span>; <span title="fa">سمفونی فانتاستیک</span>; <span title="ka">ფანტასტიკური სიმფონია</span>; <span title="hy">Ֆանտաստիկ սիմֆոնիա</span></span>

<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 movements
<dl><dd>I. <i>Rêveries – Passions</i>. Largo – Allegro agitato e appassionato assai – Religiosamente
</dd><dd>II. <i>Un bal</i>. Valse. Allegro non troppo
</dd><dd>III. <i>Scène aux champs</i>. Adagio
</dd><dd>IV. <i>Marche au supplice</i>. Allegretto non troppo
</dd><dd>V. <i>Songe d’une nuit de sabbat</i>. Larghetto – Allegro
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
